```python
db.execute("""
SELECT L.ID, L.Date, L.HGB, P.Birthday, E."Examination Date", E.Diagnosis
FROM Laboratory AS L
JOIN Patient AS P ON P.ID = L.ID
JOIN Examination AS E ON E.ID = L.ID AND E."Examination Date" = L.Date
WHERE L.HGB = (SELECT MAX(HGB) FROM Laboratory)
ORDER BY L.ID, L.Date
```
```python
LIMIT 10;
```
```python
""")
```

```python
       CAST(strftime('%Y', 'now') AS INTEGER) - CAST(strftime('%Y', P.Birthday) AS INTEGER) AS age
```

Use these structural patterns as checks. They contain no evaluation schemas, values, or answers.
- Aggregate at the requested entity grain: For per-entity totals, averages, minima, or maxima, aggregate at the entity level first, then rank or limit the aggregated result. Do not rank individual detail rows when the question asks about an entity total.

```python
db.execute("""
```
```python
SELECT COUNT(*) AS meeting_events
FROM (
  SELECT a.link_to_event
  FROM attendance AS a
  JOIN event AS e
    ON a.link_to_event = e.event_id
  WHERE e.type = 'Meeting'
  GROUP BY a.link_to_event
  HAVING COUNT(a.link_to_event) > 10
) AS sub;
""")
```

🤖 model turn:

I’ll test the exact query before submitting it.
```python
sql = """
WITH yearly AS (
    SELECT
        c.Segment,
        ym.CustomerID,
        SUM(ym.Consumption) AS total_consumption
    FROM yearmonth AS ym
    JOIN customers AS c
      ON ym.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
    WHERE c.Currency = 'CZK'
      AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM')
      AND substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013'
    GROUP BY c.Segment, ym.CustomerID
),
lowest AS (
    SELECT
        Segment,
        MIN(total_consumption) AS min_consumption
    FROM yearly
    GROUP BY Segment
),
segment_avg AS (
    SELECT
        y.Segment,
        AVG(y.total_consumption) AS annual_avg_consumption
    FROM yearly AS y
    JOIN lowest AS l
      ON y.Segment = l.Segment
     AND y.total_consumption = l.min_consumption
    GROUP BY y.Segment
)
SELECT
    MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'SME' THEN annual_avg_consumption END)
      - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'LAM' THEN annual_avg_consumption END) AS SME_LAM,
    MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'LAM' THEN annual_avg_consumption END)
      - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'KAM' THEN annual_avg_consumption END) AS LAM_KAM,
    MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'KAM' THEN annual_avg_consumption END)
      - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'SME' THEN annual_avg_consumption END) AS KAM_SME
FROM segment_avg;
"""
db.execute(sql)
```

```python
db.execute("""
WITH yearly AS (
    SELECT
        c.Segment,
        ym.CustomerID,
        SUM(ym.Consumption) AS total_consumption
    FROM yearmonth AS ym
    JOIN customers AS c
      ON ym.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
    WHERE c.Currency = 'CZK'
      AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM')
      AND substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013'
    GROUP BY c.Segment, ym.CustomerID
),
lowest AS (
    SELECT
        Segment,
        MIN(total_consumption) AS min_consumption
    FROM yearly
    GROUP BY Segment
),
segment_avg AS (
    SELECT
        y.Segment,
        AVG(y.total_consumption) AS annual_avg_consumption
    FROM yearly AS y
    JOIN lowest AS l
      ON y.Segment = l.Segment
     AND y.total_consumption = l.min_consumption
    GROUP BY y.Segment
)
SELECT
    MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'SME' THEN annual_avg_consumption END)
      - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'LAM' THEN annual_avg_consumption END) AS SME_LAM,
    MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'LAM' THEN annual_avg_consumption END)
      - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'KAM' THEN annual_avg_consumption END) AS LAM_KAM,
    MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'KAM' THEN annual_avg_consumption END)
      - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'SME' THEN annual_avg_consumption END) AS KAM_SME
FROM segment_avg;
```

```python
db.execute("""
WITH seg_year AS (
  SELECT
    c.Segment,
    substr(y.Date, 1, 4) AS yr,
    SUM(y.Consumption) AS consumption
  FROM yearmonth AS y
  JOIN customers AS c
    ON y.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  WHERE c.Currency = 'EUR'
    AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM')
    AND substr(y.Date, 1, 4) IN ('2012', '2013')
  GROUP BY c.Segment, substr(y.Date, 1, 4)
),
pct AS (
  SELECT
    y2013.Segment,
    ((y2013.consumption - y2012.consumption) / y2013.consumption) * 100.0 AS pct_increase
  FROM seg_year AS y2013
  JOIN seg_year AS y2012
    ON y2013.Segment = y2012.Segment
  WHERE y2013.yr = '2013'
    AND y2012.yr = '2012'
)
SELECT * FROM (
  SELECT 'biggest' AS rank_type, Segment, pct_increase
  FROM pct
  ORDER BY pct_increase DESC
  LIMIT 1
)
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM (
  SELECT 'lowest' AS rank_type, Segment, pct_increase
  FROM pct
  ORDER BY pct_increase ASC
  LIMIT 1
);
""")
```

```python
db.execute("""
WITH customer_totals AS (
  SELECT
    t.CustomerID,
    SUM(t.Price) AS total_price,
    SUM(t.Amount) AS total_amount,
    c.Currency
  FROM transactions_1k AS t
  INNER JOIN customers AS c
    ON t.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  GROUP BY t.CustomerID, c.Currency
)
SELECT
  CustomerID,
  total_price / total_amount AS average_price_per_single_item,
  Currency
FROM customer_totals
ORDER BY total_price DESC
LIMIT 1;
""")
```

SIMILAR SOLVED EXAMPLES (different databases — copy the SQL *style* and output-column conventions, not the table names):

  Q: Calculate the difference between the total number of students and the number of international international students in Univeristy of Tokyo from 2011 to 2014.
  Hint: international students refers to DIVIDE(MULTIPLY(num_students, pct_international_students), 100); difference refers to SUBTRACT(SUM(num_students), SUM(DIVIDE(MULTIPLY(num_students, pct_international_students), 100))); in University of Tokyo refers to university_name = 'University of Tokyo'; from 2011 to 2014 refers to year BETWEEN 2011 AND 2014
  SQL: SELECT SUM(T1.num_students) - SUM(CAST(T1.num_students * T1.pct_international_students AS REAL) / 100) FROM university_year AS T1 INNER JOIN university AS T2 ON T1.university_id = T2.id WHERE T1.year BETWEEN 2011 AND 2014 AND T2.university_name = 'University of Tokyo'
